 The Sri Lanka Armed Services Long Service Medal 
IT is hereby notified that His Excellency the President of the Democratic Socialist Republic of Sri Lanka and the Commander 
in Chief of the Armed Forces have been pleased to approve the award of the Sri Lanka Armed Services Long Service Medal 
to the persons specified in the schedule here.
                      
By Order of the Hon. President,
                                                                  
 General Kamal Gunaratne (retd) 
 WWV RWP RSP USP ndc psc Mphil
 Secretary,
 Ministry of Defence.
   
Ministry of Defence,
Colombo.  
26th July 2023.
